# Printing the Linked List Alternatively

```cpp
void printAlternatively(Node* head) {
    Node* temp = head;
    while (temp) {
        cout << temp->data << '\t'; // Print current node
        if (temp->next == nullptr) break; // If next is null, stop
        temp = temp->next->next; // Move two steps ahead
    }
    cout << endl;

}
```

create a dummy node
create a tail pointer initially
pointing to dummy

while(list1 && list2):
    if list1->val <= list2->val:
        tail-next = list1
        list1 = list1->next
    else:
        tail->next = list2
        list2 = list2->next

// connect to the tail to the non-empty node
if(list1):
    tail->next = list1
if(list2):
    tail->next = list2

return dumy->next ^CpvYpm6b

Merge Two Sorted List ^je2tTAio
